<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружный.html>дру́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drúžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружно.html>дру́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drúžno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-дру́жно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дружне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-дру́жно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дружне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>amicably, in a friendly manner</li>
<li>simultaneously, hand in hand, (everybody) together, in a concerted effort</li></ol>

</p>

***дружный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружный.html>дру́жный</a> (7024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*družьnъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drugъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friend, companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружный.html>дру́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drúžnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дружне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дружне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>friendly, amicable, personable</li>
<li>harmonious, concurrent, unanimous</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жба</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drúžba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружеский.html>дру́жеский</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drúžeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрыхнуть.html>дры́хнуть</a> (11893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрыхнуть.html>дры́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drýxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sleep
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  Дарья Аркадьевна Донцова (Darya Arkadyevna Dontsova,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:фанера.html>Фане́ра</a> Милосская: <a href = vnd.unilang:роман.html>рома́н</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:продюсер.html>Продю́сер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:козий.html>ко́зьей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рды</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрыхнуть.html>дры́хнешь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:засмеяться.html>засмея́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тетка.html>тётка</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>вторы́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сутки.html>су́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a>!</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Drýxnešʹ</b> kak surók, — zasmejálasʹ tjótka, — vtorýje sútki pošlí!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You're <b>sleeping</b> like a log <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">literally, a marmot</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, the auntie laughed - it's the second day now!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрыхнуть.html>дры́х</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3°a[(5)](6).      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — задрыхнуть.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дрых-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дряблый.html>дря́блый</a> (16052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дря́бнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drjábnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become flabby</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дрябь</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drjabʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flabbiness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dręb-</i>.Per Vasmer, quoting Mikloshich, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">drìbti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to trickle, to drip with thick drops</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">drimbù</i>), <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">drabnùs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">dramblỹs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thick-chested; elephant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Apparently also related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θρόμβος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thrómbos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θρομβεῖον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thrombeîon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дряблый.html>дря́блый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drjáblyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дрябле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дрябле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> flabby, flaccid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> weak-willed, spineless</li></ol>

<p><b>дря́б<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дряб-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-л</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***дрянь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a> (4975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1731. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дрань</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dranʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьranь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьranъ</i>, past passive participle of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьrati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tear, flay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drjanʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дря́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дря́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дря́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rubbish, trash
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><b>1929 – 1940</b>, М. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Булгаков, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>Ма́стер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маргарит.html>Маргари́та</a></i> :<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>Пошёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:купаться.html>купа́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> москва́-ре́ку, <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> попя́тили <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мо́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одежа.html>одёжу</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оставить.html>оста́вили</a>!</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pošól ja kupátʹsja na Moskvá-réku, nu i popjátili móju odjóžu, a étu <b>drjanʹ</b> ostávili!</i></dd></dl><ul><li><b>1979</b> translation by Richard Pevear, Larissa Volokhonsky<dl><dd>I went for a swim in the Moscow River, so they filched my clothes and left me this <b>trash</b>!</dd></dl></li></ul></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rotter, skunk, dirty dog</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка). <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:скверный.html>скве́рный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дря́ней</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дрянь-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***дуб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a> (4023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dǫbъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰanw-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dub</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>ду́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дубы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дубо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>oak <i>(Quercus)</i> (tree and wood)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возле.html>во́зле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>растёт</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vózle náševo doma rastjót <b>dub</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">An <i>oak</i> grows near my house.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> вирги́нский</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> virgínskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">live oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> лавроли́стный</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> lavrolístnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">laurel oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каменный.html>ка́менный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> kámennyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">holm oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скальный.html>ска́льный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> skálʹnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">durmast oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бархатный.html>ба́рхатный</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бархатистый.html>бархати́стый</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> bárxatnyj, <b>dub</b> barxatístyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Quercus_velutina" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Quercus velutina"><i>Quercus velutina</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/yellow-bark_oak" class="extiw" title="w:yellow-bark oak">yellow-bark oak</a>, quercitron, black oak, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/dyer%27s_oak" class="extiw" title="w:dyer | s oak">dyer's oak</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мореный.html>морёный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">morjónyj <b>dub</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fumed oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробковый.html>про́бковый</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> próbkovyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cork oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:австрийский.html>австри́йский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> avstríjskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Quercus cerris</i>) Turkey oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:американский.html>америка́нский</a> шарла́ховый</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> amerikánskij šarláxovyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Quercus coccinea</i>) red oak, scarlet oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> аракси́нский</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> araksínskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Quercus_araxina" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Quercus araxina"><i>Quercus araxina</i></a></span> ⇒ <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Quercus_infectoria_subsp._veneris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Quercus infectoria subsp. veneris"><i>Quercus infectoria</i> subsp. <i>veneris</i></a></span>) Aleppo oak, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cyprus_oak" class="extiw" title="w:Cyprus oak">Cyprus oak</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asian_holly_oak" class="extiw" title="w:Asian holly oak">Asian holly oak</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лый</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> bélyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Quercus alba</i>) white oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:болотный.html>боло́тный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> bolótnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Quercus palustris</i>) swamp oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голый.html>го́лый</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> gólyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Quercus_laevis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Quercus laevis"><i>Quercus laevis</i></a></span>) turkey oak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> górnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Quercus_montana" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Quercus montana"><i>Quercus montana</i></a></span>) chestnut oak, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/rock_oak" class="extiw" title="w:rock oak">rock oak</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b> до́льчатый</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dub</b> dólʹčatyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Quercus_lobata" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Quercus lobata"><i>Quercus lobata</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/valley_oak" class="extiw" title="w:valley oak">valley oak</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>вели́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> дупля́ст, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мал</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровый.html>здоро́в</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">velík <b>dub</b>, da dupljást, a mal <b>dub</b>, da zdoróv</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">size or greatness is not always good</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">the oak is large but it has hollows, while the other one is small but healthy</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изготовленный.html>изгото́влен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>ду́ба</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot stol izgotóvlen iz <b>dúba</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">This table is made from oak</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tan, bark of an oak or other tree used to obtain tannic acid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>ду́ба</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ <b>dúba</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kick the bucket, to die</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rаre</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boat made from oak boards or a single oak-tree trunk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stupid man, blockhead, numskull
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>Како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakoj že ty <b>dub</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a blockhead are you!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>ду́ба</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дубо́в</a></i>).

<p><b>ду<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бо́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дубок.html>дубо́к</a> (20489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуб.html>дуб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dub</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дубок.html>дубо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dubók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дубок.html>дубка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дубок.html>дубки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дубок.html>дубко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>oaklet, oakling, young oak</li></ol>

***дуга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>дуга́</a> (6720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>дуга́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">duga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rainbow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dǫga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rainbow, semicircle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>дуга́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dugá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>дуги́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>ду́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>ду́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>arc, arch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electricity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> arc
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электрический.html>электри́ческая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуга.html>дуга́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">elektríčeskaja <b>dugá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">electrical <b>arc</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bow, curve, rib</li>
<li>shaft bow <i>(of a harness)</i></li></ol>

***дудка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>дудка</a> (11858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дуда́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dudá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fife, pipe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Miklosich and Berneker considered this Slavic word to be borrowed from Turkic, but Vasmer and Brückner believe that the close sound rendition of these onomatopoetic words is a "mere chance". Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">daudýtė</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">panpipe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>ду́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúdka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дудка.html>ду́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дудка.html>ду́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дудка.html>ду́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fife, pipe <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small shrill pipe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плясать.html>пляса́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> чью́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дудка.html>ду́дку</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pljasátʹ pod čʹjú-libo <b>dúdku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dance to somebody's tune / piping</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дудка.html>ду́дки</a>!</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dúdki!</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not on your life!, fudge!, rats!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">interjection</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ду́д<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

***дуля.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуля.html>ду́ля</a> (19453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">гду́ля</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gdúlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">гду́ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gdúnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъduňa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cydōnia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Κυδωνία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kudōnía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quince-tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуля.html>ду́ля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúlja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуля.html>ду́ль</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> small pear</li>
<li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fig_sign" class="extiw" title="w:Fig sign">fig sign</a> (a rude gesture in which the hand makes a fist and the thumb is stuck between the index and middle fingers); indicates "nothing for you", "nuts to you"</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Not the same vulgar meaning that this gesture has in Western European countries such as Germany.
</p>

***дума.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дума.html>ду́ма</a> (2454)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thought, care, council</span><span title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span>, possibly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōmaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">judicial decision, act, thought</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌳𐍉𐌼𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dōms</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span lang="got">𐌳𐍉𐌼𐌹𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dōmian</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to judge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌳𐍉𐌼</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dōm</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">council, thought</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also compare modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">-tum</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-dom</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doom</i>.

***думать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a> (107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dumati</i>, a loan from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dōmijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to judge, think</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deem</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúmatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подумать.html>поду́мать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to think</li>
<li>to believe, to suppose</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думаться.html>ду́маться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúmatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подуматься.html>поду́маться</a></b>)
</p>
